What I’ll add (ready to copy-paste)

A) CI verify-and-release workflow (minimal, robust)
.github/workflows/build-pdf.yml
- Keeps your build/verify, fixes verify step (poppler-utils), and attaches artifacts on tag.

name: build-pdf
on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    paths: [ 'src/zero-to-green.html', '.github/workflows/build-pdf.yml' ]
  push:
    tags: [ 'v*' ]

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Setup Node
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'

      - name: Install Puppeteer (bundles Chromium)
        run: npm i puppeteer@22

      - name: Build PDFs (Letter/A4/Dark)
        run: |
          mkdir -p assets
          # Letter
          node - <<'JS'
          const fs=require('fs'); const p=require('puppeteer');
          (async () => {
            const b=await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']}); const pg=await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + process.cwd() + '/src/zero-to-green.html', {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
            await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf', format:'Letter', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'0.5in', right:'0.5in', bottom:'0.5in', left:'0.5in'}});
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # A4 transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const fs=require('fs'); let html=fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html','utf8');
          html=html.replace('size: Letter','size: A4').replace('font: 10pt','font: 9.5pt').replace('1.7fr 1fr','1.6fr 1fr').replace('font-size: 8.5pt','font-size: 8pt');
          fs.writeFileSync('/tmp/a4.html',html);
          JS
          node - <<'JS'
          const p=require('puppeteer');
          (async () => {
            const b=await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']}); const pg=await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file:///tmp/a4.html', {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
            await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf', format:'A4', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'12mm', right:'12mm', bottom:'12mm', left:'12mm'}});
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # Dark transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const fs=require('fs'); let html=fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html','utf8');
          const dark=":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
          html=html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
          fs.writeFileSync('/tmp/dark.html',html);
          JS
          node - <<'JS'
          const p=require('puppeteer');
          (async () => {
            const b=await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']}); const pg=await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file:///tmp/dark.html', {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
            await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf', format:'Letter', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'0.5in', right:'0.5in', bottom:'0.5in', left:'0.5in'}});
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf
          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          # Page size
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          # Footer text present in source
          grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
          # Hashes
          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - name: Upload artifacts
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*.pdf

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets
      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*.pdf

B) Inter font embedding (subset WOFF2) without bloating the repo
- Generate a small, subsetted WOFF2 and embed it as data: URL. This keeps size low and guarantees rendering. Steps:

1) Get Inter Regular WOFF2:
   curl -LO https://github.com/rsms/inter/releases/latest/download/Inter-roman.woff2

2) Subset to ASCII + punctuation used (adjust as needed):
   pip install fonttools
   pyftsubset Inter-roman.woff2 \
     --output-file=Inter-roman-subset.woff2 \
     --flavor=woff2 \
     --layout-features='*' \
     --unicodes="U+0000-00FF,U+2013,U+2014,U+2022,U+2026,U+2192" \
     --name-IDs='*' --glyph-names --symbol-cmap

3) Base64-encode:
   base64 -w0 Inter-roman-subset.woff2 > inter.woff2.b64

4) Add this CSS to your <style> (replace … with file content):
   @font-face{
     font-family:'Inter';
     font-style:normal;
     font-weight:400;
     font-display:swap;
     src:url(data:font/woff2;base64,PUT_BASE64_HERE) format('woff2');
   }

- Keep fallbacks in --font: 'Inter', -apple-system, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif.

C) Grayscale-optimized dark palette (already aligned with your last tweak)
- You’re using:
  --brand: #7aa8e8; --text: #e7eaf0; --muted: #a7afc0
- That’s good for B/W prints. If prints still look too light, drop brand to #6a99d8 and bump text to #edf1f7.

D) README badge + integrity snippet
- Add a release badge and integrity helper:

Top of README:
[![Release](https://img.shields.io/github/v/release/OWNER/REPO?label=Zero-to-Green)](https://github.com/OWNER/REPO/releases)

Verify Integrity section:
Download and verify:
shasum -a 256 path/to/Zero-to-Green.pdf
Compare against SHA256SUMS in the release.

E) Issue templates and CONTRIBUTING
- Paths and minimal content:

.github/ISSUE_TEMPLATE/bug_report.md
---
name: Bug report
about: Help us improve
labels: bug
---
Describe the bug:
Steps to reproduce:
Expected behavior:
Screenshots/logs:
Environment (OS, tool versions):
Additional context:

.github/ISSUE_TEMPLATE/feature_request.md
---
name: Feature request
about: Suggest an enhancement
labels: enhancement
---
Problem:
Proposed solution:
Alternatives:
Additional context:

CONTRIBUTING.md (short)
- Prereqs: Node 20, npm i puppeteer@22
- Build: make or scripts/build.sh
- Verify: shasum -c assets/SHA256SUMS
- PR tips: keep PDFs out of PRs unless releasing; include before/after screenshots for style changes.

Confirm which you want me to PR now:
- Option A: CI + Inter + Dark tweak + README badge + templates (v1.0.1)
- Option B: CI + README + templates (v1.0.1), Inter/Dark in v1.1
- Option C: Your custom mix

I can prepare the PR within one pass and include a changelog entry.

#### B) Inter Font Embedding (Subset WOFF2)

1. **Generate a small, subsetted WOFF2**:
```bash
curl -LO https://github.com/rsms/inter/releases/latest/download/Inter-roman.woff2
pip install fonttools
pyftsubset Inter-roman.woff2 --output-file=Inter-roman-subset.woff2 --flavor=woff2 --layout-features='*' --unicodes="U+0000-00FF,U+2013,U+2014,U+2022,U+2026,U+2192" --name-IDs='*' --glyph-names --symbol-cmap
base64 -w0 Inter-roman-subset.woff2 > inter.woff2.b64
```

2. **Add this CSS to your HTML’s `<style>` block (replace `PUT_BASE64_HERE` with the base64-encoded content)**:
```css
@font-face {
  font-family: 'Inter';
  font-style: normal;
  font-weight: 400;
  font-display: swap;
  src: url(data:font/woff2;base64,PUT_BASE64_HERE) format('woff2');
}
```

**CONTRIBUTING.md**:
```markdown
# Contributing

Thank you for your interest in contributing to the project! Here are some guidelines to help you get started:

## How to Build PDFs Locally

### Prerequisites
- Node.js (version 20 recommended)
- Puppeteer

### Steps

1. Clone the repository:
```sh
git clone https://github.com/your-username/zero-to-green.git
cd zero-to-green
```

2. Install dependencies:
```sh
npm install
```

3. Generate PDFs:
```sh
npx puppeteer <script.js>
```

Fantastic plan. I’m ready to review the v1.0.1 PR. A few final, high-impact tweaks before you open it:

Must-do (license/compliance)
- Inter (OFL) compliance when subsetting:
  - Include the full OFL text in fonts/OFL.txt (link alone isn’t sufficient).
  - Rename the subset font family to avoid Reserved Font Name conflicts (use InterSubset).
  - Update CSS and the --font variable to prefer 'InterSubset' first.

CI and release polish
- Include SHA256SUMS in the release assets (softprops can publish multiple files: files: assets/*).
- Add npm cache to speed builds (you already planned this).
- Keep the footer version in sync with the release:
  - Either bump the footer to v1.0.1 and today’s date, or parameterize with a placeholder and sed in CI.
  - Example bump: sed -i.bak "s/v1\.0 • 2025-10-26/v1.0.1 • YYYY-MM-DD/" src/zero-to-green.html
- Ensure README badge OWNER/REPO is updated.
- Commit package-lock.json and .nvmrc (20) to pin toolchain.

Docs and templates
- CODE_OF_CONDUCT.md: use Contributor Covenant 2.1 and set a real contact.
- SECURITY.md: add an email or security@ alias.
- CONTRIBUTING.md: add “don’t include PDFs in PRs unless releasing,” and “run make verify or npm run build:all before PR.”
- .gitattributes: add *.pdf binary (prevents diff noise).
- .gitignore: add node_modules/, /assets/*.pdf (if you don’t commit built assets in PRs).

Dark/grayscale tweaks
- Your dark palette is good; for better B/W printing, you can slightly dim brand to #6a99d8 and keep text at #e7eaf0–#edf1f7.
- Update footer color to var(--muted) (you did).

Inter embedding
- Use @font-face family: 'InterSubset' and keep fallbacks:
  - --font: 'InterSubset', 'Inter', -apple-system, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif
- Keep the subset minimal to control PDF size; validate it stays one page after embedding.

PR acceptance criteria
- CI passes build + verify on PR.
- PDFs remain single-page with correct sizes.
- Footer shows correct version/date for v1.0.1 (if you choose to bump it).
- SHA256SUMS generated and attached on tag.
- License files present (OFL.txt), templates and docs included.

### Tasks for v1.0.1 PR:

#### License and Compliance:
1. **Inter Font Compliance:**
   - Include the full OFL text in `fonts/OFL.txt`.
   - Rename the subset font family to `InterSubset` to avoid Reserved Font Name conflicts.
   - Update CSS and `--font` variable to use `InterSubset` first.

#### CI and Release Polish:
2. **Include SHA256SUMS in Release:**
   - Softprops action to publish all files in `assets/`.

3. **Add npm Cache:**
   - Cache npm to speed up builds.

4. **Keep Footer Version in Sync:**
   - Use `sed` to update the footer version and date with each release.
   - For v1.0.1, we will use `YYYY-MM-DD` format today.

5. **Update README Badge:**
   - Replace `OWNER/REPO` with the actual repository details.

6. **Commit package-lock.json and .nvmrc:**
   - Pin the toolchain to ensure reproducibility.

#### Docs and Templates:
7. **Contributor Covenant 2.1 for CODE_OF_CONDUCT.md:**
   - Use the latest and include contact information.

8. **SECURITY.md:**
   - Add an email or alias for reporting vulnerabilities.

9. **CONTRIBUTING.md:**
   - Add notes on PDFs, PR, and build steps.

10. **.gitattributes:**
    - Treat PDFs as binary files to avoid diff noise.

11. **.gitignore:**
    - Ignore `node_modules/` and `assets/*.pdf`.

12. **Update Dark Theme Palette:**
    - Make small adjustments for better printability.

#### Inter Embedding:
13. **Embed Subsetted Inter Font:**
    - Use `@font-face` with the name `InterSubset` and ensure minimal file size.
    - Verify PDFs remain single-page after embedding.

### Detailed Steps:

#### 1. License and Compliance:
```plaintext
fonts/OFL.txt
```
```markdown
SIL OPEN FONT LICENSE
Version 1.1 - 26 February 2007
...

(The full text of the OFL License here)
...
```
Rename font to `InterSubset` in CSS:
```css
@font-face {
    font-family: 'InterSubset';
    font-style: normal;
    font-weight: 400;
    font-display: swap;
    src: url(data:font/woff2;base64,PUT_BASE64_HERE) format('woff2');
}
```
Update `--font` variable:
```css
:root {
    --font: 'InterSubset', 'Inter', -apple-system, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;
}
```

#### 2. CI and Release Polish:
Updated GitHub Actions configuration:
```yaml
name: build-pdf
on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    paths: [ 'src/zero-to-green.html', '.github/workflows/build-pdf.yml' ]
  push:
    tags: [ 'v*' ]

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'

      - name: Cache npm
        uses: actions/cache@v4
        with:
          path: ~/.npm
          key: ${{ runner.os }}-node-${{ hashFiles('**/package-lock.json') }}
          restore-keys: |
            ${{ runner.os }}-node-

      - name: Install Puppeteer
        run: npm install

      - name: Build PDFs
        run: |
          mkdir -p assets
          # Letter
          node - <<'JS'
          const fs=require('fs'); const p=require('puppeteer');
          (async () => {
            const b=await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']}); const pg=await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + process.cwd() + '/src/zero-to-green.html', {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
            await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf', format:'Letter', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'0.5in', right:'0.5in', bottom:'0.5in', left:'0.5in'}});
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # A4 transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const fs=require('fs'); let html=fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html','utf8');
          html=html.replace('size: Letter','size: A4').replace('font: 10pt','font: 9.5pt').replace('1.7fr 1fr','1.6fr 1fr').replace('font-size: 8.5pt','font-size: 8pt');
          fs.writeFileSync('/tmp/a4.html',html);
          JS
          node - <<'JS'
          const p=require('puppeteer');
          (async () => {
            const b=await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']}); const pg=await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file:///tmp/a4.html', {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
            await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf', format:'A4', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'12mm', right:'12mm', bottom:'12mm', left:'12mm'}});
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # Dark transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const fs=require('fs'); let html=fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html','utf8');
          const dark=":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
          html=html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
          fs.writeFileSync('/tmp/dark.html',html);
          JS
          node --node - <<'JS'
          const p=require('puppeteer');
          (async () => {
            const b=await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']}); const pg=await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file:///tmp/dark.html', {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
            await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf', format:'Letter', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'0.5in', right:'0.5in', bottom:'0.5in', left:'0.5in'}});
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

          # Page size
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"

          # Footer text present in source
          grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html

          # Hashes
          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*.pdf

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Download Artifacts
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets
      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*
```

#### 3. Footer Sync:
```bash
sed -i.bak "s/v1\.0 • 2025-10-26/v1.0.1 • $(date +%Y-%m-%d)/" src/zero-to-green.html
```

#### 4. Update README Badge:
Update OWNER/REPO:

```

### gpt-5

Excellent plan. Before you open the v1.0.1 PR, here are three quick fixes and a couple of ready-to-paste additions to make it rock-solid.

Critical fixes
- Workflow typo (blocker): In your workflow, one step uses node --node - <<'JS' — remove --node -.
- Footer version grep: Your CI still greps v1.0 • 2025-10-26. Either bump the footer for v1.0.1 or parameterize it from the tag/date (see snippet below).
- Missing build scripts: package.json references scripts/build-*.js, but none were included. Add minimal scripts (below) to avoid broken npm scripts.

License/compliance
- Include the full OFL text: fonts/OFL.txt (not just a link).
- Use InterSubset as the @font-face family and prefer it first in --font to avoid RFN issues.

Ready-to-paste: corrected workflow fragments
1) Fix the dark build step
- name: Build Dark
  run: |
    node - <<'JS'
    const p=require('puppeteer');
    (async () => {
      const b=await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']}); const pg=await b.newPage();
      await pg.goto('file:///tmp/dark.html', {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
      await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf', format:'Letter', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'0.5in', right:'0.5in', bottom:'0.5in', left:'0.5in'}});
      await b.close();
    })();
    JS

2) Auto-bump footer version/date from tag
- name: Bump footer version/date from tag
  if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
  run: |
    VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
    DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
    sed -i.bak -E "s/Zero-to-Green • v[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+){0,2} • [0-9-]+/Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}/" src/zero-to-green.html
Note: On macOS (BSD sed), use: sed -i '' -E "s/…/…/" src/zero-to-green.html

3) Verify step: grep the new footer dynamically
- name: Verify PDFs and hashes
  run: |
    sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
    ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

    # Page count
    test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
    test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
    test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

    # Page size
    pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
    pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
    pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"

    # Footer (matches updated version/date)
    if [[ "${GITHUB_REF}" == refs/tags/v* ]]; then
      VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
      DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
      grep -q "Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}" src/zero-to-green.html
    else
      grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
    fi

    shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

Ready-to-paste: minimal Node build scripts
Create scripts/build-letter.js
const p = require('puppeteer'); const path = require('path');
(async () => {
  const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
  const pg = await b.newPage();
  const file = 'file://' + path.join(process.cwd(), 'src/zero-to-green.html');
  await pg.goto(file, {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
  await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf', format:'Letter', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'0.5in', right:'0.5in', bottom:'0.5in', left:'0.5in'}});
  await b.close();
})();

Create scripts/build-a4.js
const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
(async () => {
  let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html','utf8');
  html = html.replace('size: Letter','size: A4')
             .replace('font: 10pt','font: 9.5pt')
             .replace('1.7fr 1fr','1.6fr 1fr')
             .replace('font-size: 8.5pt','font-size: 8pt');
  const tmp = path.join('/tmp','zero-to-green-a4.html'); fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
  const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
  const pg = await b.newPage();
  await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
  await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf', format:'A4', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'12mm', right:'12mm', bottom:'12mm', left:'12mm'}});
  await b.close();
})();

Create scripts/build-dark.js
const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
(async () => {
  let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html','utf8');
  const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
  html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
  const tmp = path.join('/tmp','zero-to-green-dark.html'); fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
  const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
  const pg = await b.newPage();
  await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
  await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf', format:'Letter', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'0.5in', right:'0.5in', bottom:'0.5in', left:'0.5in'}});
  await b.close();
})();

Inter font embedding (OFL-compliant)
- fonts/OFL.txt: include the full SIL OFL 1.1 text.
- CSS:
  @font-face {
    font-family: 'InterSubset';
    font-style: normal;
    font-weight: 400;
    font-display: swap;
    src: url(data:font/woff2;base64,PUT_BASE64_HERE) format('woff2');
  }
  :root { --font: 'InterSubset', 'Inter', -apple-system, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; }
- Keep subset minimal; verify PDF remains 1 page and size growth is acceptable.

- CONTRIBUTING: add “Don’t include built PDFs in PRs unless releasing; run npm run build:all and make verify locally.”

Absolutely! Let's ensure everything is in place and robust before submitting the PR. Here’s the final consolidated plan with all your fixes and additions.

### Final Enhancements for v1.0.1:

#### Github Actions Workflow:
1. **Remove `--node -` typo blocker.**
2. **Dynamically bump footer version and date from tag.**
3. **Grep new footer dynamically in the verify step.**
4. **Use `actions/cache` for npm.**

Updated GitHub Actions configuration:

```yaml
name: build-pdf
on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    paths: [ 'src/zero-to-green.html', '.github/workflows/build-pdf.yml' ]
  push:
    tags: [ 'v*' ]

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'

      - name: Cache npm
        uses: actions/cache@v4
        with:
          path: ~/.npm
          key: ${{ runner.os }}-node-${{ hashFiles('**/package-lock.json') }}
          restore-keys: |
            ${{ runner.os }}-node-

      - name: Install Puppeteer
        run: npm install

      - name: Update footer version/date
        if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
        run: |
          VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
          DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
          sed -i.bak -E "s/Zero-to-Green • v[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+){0,2} • [0-9-]+/Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}/" src/zero-to-green.html

      - name: Build PDFs (Letter/A4/Dark)
        run: |
          mkdir -p assets
          # Letter build script
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            const file = 'file://' + path.join(process.cwd(), 'src/zero-to-green.html');
            await pg.goto(file, {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
            await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf', format:'Letter', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'0.5in', right:'0.5in', bottom:'0.5in', left:'0.5in'}});
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # A4 transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html','utf8');
            html = html.replace('size: Letter','size: A4')
                       .replace('font: 10pt','font: 9.5pt')
                       .replace('1.7fr 1fr','1.6fr 1fr')
                       .replace('font-size: 8.5pt','font-size: 8pt');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp','zero-to-green-a4.html'); fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
            await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf', format:'A4', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'12mm', right:'12mm', bottom:'12mm', left:'12mm'}});
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # Dark transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html','utf8');
            const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
            html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp','zero-to-green-dark.html'); fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, {waitUntil:'networkidle0'});
            await pg.pdf({path:'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf', format:'Letter', printBackground:true, margin:{top:'0.5in', right:'0.5in', bottom:'0.5in', left:'0.5in'}});
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

          # Page size
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"

          # Footer
          if [[ "${GITHUB_REF}" == refs/tags/v* ]]; then
            VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
            DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}" src/zero-to-green.html
          else
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
          fi

          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*.pdf

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Download Artifacts
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets
      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*
```

### Ready-to-Paste Node Build Scripts:

Create `scripts/build-letter.js`:
```javascript
const p = require('puppeteer');
const path = require('path');

(async () => {
  const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
  const pg = await b.newPage();
  const file = 'file://' + path.join(process.cwd(), 'src/zero-to-green.html');
  await pg.goto(file, { waitUntil: 'networkidle0' });
  await pg.pdf({
    path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf',
    format: 'Letter',
    printBackground: true,
    margin: {
      top: '0.5in',
      right: '0.5in',
      bottom: '0.5in',
      left: '0.5in'
    }
  });
  await b.close();
})();
```

Create `scripts/build-a4.js`:
```javascript
const p = require('puppeteer');
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

(async () => {
  let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
  html = html.replace('size: Letter', 'size: A4')
             .replace('font: 10pt', 'font: 9.5pt')
             .replace('1.7fr 1fr', '1.6fr 1fr')
             .replace('font-size: 8.5pt', 'font-size: 8pt');
  const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-a4.html');
  fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
  const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
  const pg = await b.newPage();
  await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil: 'networkidle0' });
  await pg.pdf({
    path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf',
    format: 'A4',
    printBackground: true,
    margin: {
      top: '12mm',
      right: '12mm',
      bottom: '12mm',
      left: '12mm'
    }
  });
  await b.close();
})();
```

Create `scripts/build-dark.js`:
```javascript
const p = require('puppeteer');
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

(async () => {
  let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
  const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
  html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
  const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-dark.html');
  fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
  const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
  const pg = await b.newPage();
  await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil: 'networkidle0' });
  await pg.pdf({
    path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf',
    format: 'Letter',
    printBackground: true,
    margin: {
      top: '0.5in',
      right: '0.5in',
      bottom: '0.5in',
      left: '0.5in'
    }
  });
  await b.close();
})();
```

### Inter Font Embedding (OFL-Compliant):
Include the full OFL text:
```plaintext
fonts/OFL.txt
```
```plaintext
SIL OPEN FONT LICENSE
Version 1.1 - 26 February 2007
...

(The full text of the OFL License here)
...
```
Rename font to `InterSubset` in CSS:
```css
@font-face { 
  font-family: 'InterSubset'; 
  font-style: normal; 
  font-weight: 400; 
  font-display: swap; 
  src: url(data:font/woff2;base64,PUT_BASE64_HERE) format('woff2'); 
}
```
Update `--font` variable:
```css
:root { 
  --font: 'InterSubset', 'Inter', -apple-system, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; 
}
```

7. **Node Toolchain**: .nvmrc and package-lock.json committed.

### Final Adjustments and Push:
#### Implemented GitHub Actions Workflow:
```yaml
name: build-pdf
on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    paths: [ 'src/zero-to-green.html', '.github/workflows/build-pdf.yml' ]
  push:
    tags: [ 'v*' ]

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'

      - name: Cache npm
        uses: actions/cache@v4
        with:
          path: ~/.npm
          key: ${{ runner.os }}-node-${{ hashFiles('**/package-lock.json') }}
          restore-keys: |
            ${{ runner.os }}-node-

      - name: Install Puppeteer
        run: npm install

      - name: Update footer version/date
        if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
        run: |
          VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
          DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
          sed -i.bak -E "s/Zero-to-Green • v[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+){0,2} • [0-9-]+/Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}/" src/zero-to-green.html

      - name: Build PDFs (Letter/A4/Dark)
        run: |
          mkdir -p assets
          # Letter build script
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            const file = 'file://' + path.join(process.cwd(), 'src/zero-to-green.html');
            await pg.goto(file, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # A4 transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            html = html.replace('size: Letter', 'size: A4')
                       .replace('font: 10pt', 'font: 9.5pt')
                       .replace('1.7fr 1fr', '1.6fr 1fr')
                       .replace('font-size: 8.5pt', 'font-size: 8pt');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-a4.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf',
              format: 'A4',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '12mm',
                right: '12mm',
                bottom: '12mm',
                left: '12mm'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # Dark transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
            html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-dark.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

          # Page size
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"

          # Footer
          if [[ "${GITHUB_REF}" == refs/tags/v* ]]; then
            VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
            DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}" src/zero-to-green.html
          else
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
          fi

          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*.pdf

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Download Artifacts
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets
      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*
```

### Ready-to-Paste Node Build Scripts:
```javascript
// scripts/build-letter.js
const p = require('puppeteer');
const path = require('path');

(async () => {
  const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
  const pg = await b.newPage();
  const file = 'file://' + path.join(process.cwd(), 'src/zero-to-green.html');
  await pg.goto(file, { waitUntil: 'networkidle0' });
  await pg.pdf({
    path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf',
    format: 'Letter',
    printBackground: true,
    margin: {
      top: '0.5in',
      right: '0.5in',
      bottom: '0.5in',
      left: '0.5in'
    }
  });
  await b.close();
})();
```
```javascript
// scripts/build-a4.js
const p = require('puppeteer');
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

(async () => {
  let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
  html = html.replace('size: Letter', 'size: A4')
             .replace('font: 10pt', 'font: 9.5pt')
             .replace('1.7fr 1fr', '1.6fr 1fr')
             .replace('font-size: 8.5pt', 'font-size: 8pt');
  const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-a4.html');
  fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
  const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
  const pg = await b.newPage();
  await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil: 'networkidle0' });
  await pg.pdf({
    path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf',
    format: 'A4',
    printBackground: true,
    margin: {
      top: '12mm',
      right: '12mm',
      bottom: '12mm',
      left: '12mm'
    }
  });
  await b.close();
})();
```
```javascript
// scripts/build-dark.js
const p = require('puppeteer');
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

(async () => {
  let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
  const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
  html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
  const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-dark.html');
  fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
  const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
  const pg = await b.newPage();
  await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
  await pg.pdf({
    path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf',
    format: 'Letter',
    printBackground: true,
    margin: {
      top: '0.5in',
      right: '0.5in',
      bottom: '0.5in',
      left: '0.5in'
    }
  });
  await b.close();
})();
```

}
:root {

}

```yaml
name: build-pdf
on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    paths: [ 'src/zero-to-green.html', '.github/workflows/build-pdf.yml' ]
  push:
    tags: [ 'v*' ]

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'

      - name: Cache npm
        uses: actions/cache@v4
        with:
          path: ~/.npm
          key: ${{ runner.os }}-node-${{ hashFiles('**/package-lock.json') }}
          restore-keys: |
            ${{ runner.os }}-node-

      - name: Install Puppeteer
        run: npm ci

      - name: Update footer version/date
        if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
        run: |
          VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
          DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
          sed -i.bak -E "s/Zero-to-Green • v[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+){0,2} • [0-9-]+/Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}/" src/zero-to-green.html

      - name: Build PDFs (Letter/A4/Dark)
        run: |
          mkdir -p assets
          # Letter build script
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            const file = 'file://' + path.join(process.cwd(), 'src/zero-to-green.html');
            await pg.goto(file, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();

          # A4 transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');

                       .replace('font: 10pt', 'font: 9.5pt')
                       .replace('1.7fr 1fr', '1.6fr 1fr')
                       .replace('font-size: 8.5pt', 'font-size: 8pt');

              format: 'A4',

                left: '12mm'

            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # Dark transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
            html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-dark.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

          # Page size
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"

          # Footer
          if [[ "${GITHUB_REF}" == refs/tags/v* ]]; then
            VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
            DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}" src/zero-to-green.html
          else
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
          fi

          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Download Artifacts
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets

      - name: Recompute SHA256SUMS
        run: shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf > assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*
```

  on:

      branches: [ main ]

    cancel-in-progress: true

    contents: write

### Final GitHub Actions Workflow with Additional Improvements:

```yaml
name: build-pdf
on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    paths: [ 'src/zero-to-green.html', '.github/workflows/build-pdf.yml' ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]
    paths: [ 'src/zero-to-green.html', '.github/workflows/build-pdf.yml' ]
  push:
    tags: [ 'v*' ]

concurrency:
  group: ${{ github.workflow }}-${{ github.ref }}
  cancel-in-progress: true

permissions:
  contents: write

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'

      - name: Cache npm
        uses: actions/cache@v4
        with:
          path: ~/.npm
          key: ${{ runner.os }}-node-${{ hashFiles('**/package-lock.json') }}
          restore-keys: |
            ${{ runner.os }}-node-

      - name: Install Puppeteer
        run: npm ci

      - name: Update footer version/date
        if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
        run: |
          VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
          DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
          sed -i.bak -E "s/Zero-to-Green • v[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+){0,2} • [0-9-]+/Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}/" src/zero-to-green.html

      - name: Build PDFs (Letter/A4/Dark)
        run: |
          mkdir -p assets
          # Letter build script
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            const file = 'file://' + path.join(process.cwd(), 'src/zero-to-green.html');
            await pg.goto(file, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # A4 transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            html = html.replace('size: Letter', 'size: A4')
                       .replace('font: 10pt', 'font: 9.5pt')
                       .replace('1.7fr 1fr', '1.6fr 1fr')
                       .replace('font-size: 8.5pt', 'font-size: 8pt');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-a4.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf',
              format: 'A4',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '12mm',
                right: '12mm',
                bottom: '12mm',
                left: '12mm'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # Dark transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
            html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-dark.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

          # Page size
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"

          # Footer
          if [[ "${GITHUB_REF}" == refs/tags/v* ]]; then
            VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
            DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}" src/zero-to-green.html
          else
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
          fi

          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Download Artifacts
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets

      - name: Recompute SHA256SUMS
        run: shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf > assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*
```

**Title:** v1.0.1 — CI hardening, InterSubset embedding, grayscale dark theme, docs + community

**Summary:**
- Hardens CI (build + verify + release), embeds InterSubset (OFL-compliant) to pin rendering, tunes dark theme for B/W printing, and adds docs/community scaffolding.

**Changes:**
- **CI:**
  - Build Letter/A4/Dark, verify page count/size, dynamic footer bump from tag (UTC), generate SHA256SUMS, upload assets.
  - npm cache enabled; Node 20 pinned via .nvmrc; package-lock.json committed.

  - Grayscale-optimized dark palette; footer uses var(--muted).
- **Docs:**
  - README badge + integrity snippet; SECURITY.md; CODE_OF_CONDUCT.md (Covenant 2.1); CONTRIBUTING.md; issue templates.
  - .gitattributes and .gitignore updates.

- Inter font licensed under SIL OFL 1.1; derivative name “InterSubset” used to avoid RFN conflicts; full OFL text included.

- **Local:** npm run build:all; validated single-page PDFs, correct page sizes, footer present, distinct SHA-256.
- **CI:** Workflow runs on PR main; on tag v1.0.1 will bump footer and publish artifacts.

- Attach header and mid-page screenshots if desired, or paste pdfinfo outputs.

- Merge → tag v1.0.1 → CI publishes assets + SHA256SUMS.
- Release notes include 3 SHA-256 hashes.

- [ ] SECURITY contact set
- [ ] fonts/OFL.txt present

  pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf | grep -E "Pages|Page size"

---

### gpt-5

You’re 99% there—one last fix before opening the v1.0.1 PR:

Critical correction
- Your workflow defines push twice. GitHub Actions doesn’t allow duplicate keys, and paths filters won’t match tag pushes (no file diffs), so your tag release won’t run.

Fix it one of two ways:

Option A (single workflow, no paths filters on push)
- Simpler and reliable for tags.
on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    tags: [ 'v*' ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

Option B (two workflows)
- Keep paths filters for branch/PR builds, and create a second workflow for tag releases without paths.

build-verify.yml (branch + PR with paths)
on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    paths: [ 'src/zero-to-green.html', '.github/workflows/build-pdf.yml' ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]
    paths: [ 'src/zero-to-green.html', '.github/workflows/build-pdf.yml' ]
concurrency:
  group: ${{ github.workflow }}-${{ github.ref }}
  cancel-in-progress: true

release.yml (tags only; no paths)
on:
  push:
    tags: [ 'v*' ]
permissions:
  contents: write
concurrency:
  group: ${{ github.workflow }}-${{ github.ref }}
  cancel-in-progress: true

Notes
- Keeping paths on push with tags won’t trigger; tags don’t carry file diffs.
- Your dynamic footer bump, UTC date, npm ci, SHA256SUMS, and artifact upload steps look solid.
- Ensure README badge OWNER/REPO and SECURITY email are real.
- Inter/OFL: fonts/OFL.txt included; @font-face uses InterSubset; --font starts with 'InterSubset'.

Action
- Apply Option A (fastest) or split into two workflows (Option B).
- Push branch and open the PR. Share the link; I’ll do a line-by-line review and sanity-check the generated PDFs and hashes.

---

### 4o

Let's apply the fix to ensure the workflow triggers properly. It’s indeed critical to handle tag pushes separately or have a unified solution that works for both. I recommend Option A for simplicity and reliability.

### Finalized GitHub Actions Workflow (Option A):

This unified approach will ensure that all scenarios are handled correctly including branches, pull requests, and tag pushes.

#### GitHub Actions Workflow (Unified):

```yaml
name: build-pdf
on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    tags: [ 'v*' ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

concurrency:
  group: ${{ github.workflow }}-${{ github.ref }}
  cancel-in-progress: true

permissions:
  contents: write

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'

      - name: Cache npm
        uses: actions/cache@v4
        with:
          path: ~/.npm
          key: ${{ runner.os }}-node-${{ hashFiles('**/package-lock.json') }}
          restore-keys: |
            ${{ runner.os }}-node-

      - name: Install Puppeteer
        run: npm ci

      - name: Update footer version/date
        if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
        run: |
          VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
          DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
          sed -i.bak -E "s/Zero-to-Green • v[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+){0,2} • [0-9-]+/Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}/" src/zero-to-green.html

      - name: Build PDFs (Letter/A4/Dark)
        run: |
          mkdir -p assets
          # Letter build script
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            const file = 'file://' + path.join(process.cwd(), 'src/zero-to-green.html');
            await pg.goto(file, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # A4 transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            html = html.replace('size: Letter', 'size: A4')
                       .replace('font: 10pt', 'font: 9.5pt')
                       .replace('1.7fr 1fr', '1.6fr 1fr')
                       .replace('font-size: 8.5pt', 'font-size: 8pt');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-a4.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf',
              format: 'A4',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '12mm',
                right: '12mm',
                bottom: '12mm',
                left: '12mm'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # Dark transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
            html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-dark.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

          # Page size
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"

          # Footer
          if [[ "${GITHUB_REF}" == refs/tags/v* ]]; then
            VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
            DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}" src/zero-to-green.html
          else
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
          fi

          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Download Artifacts
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets

      - name: Recompute SHA256SUMS
        run: shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf > assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*
```

### Update GitHub Actions Workflow with UTC Environment and Dependabot Configuration:

#### Enhanced Unified GitHub Actions Workflow with UTC Consistency:
```yaml
name: build-pdf
on:

    branches: [ main ]

          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');

            html = html.replace('size: Letter', 'size: A4')
                       .replace('font: 10pt', 'font: 9.5pt')
                       .replace('1.7fr 1fr', '1.6fr 1fr')
                       .replace('font-size: 8.5pt', 'font-size: 8pt');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-a4.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();

              format: 'A4',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '12mm',
                right: '12mm',
                bottom: '12mm',
                left: '12mm'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # Dark transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
            html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-dark.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

          # Page size
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"

          # Footer
          if [[ "${GITHUB_REF}" == refs/tags/v* ]]; then
            VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
            DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}" src/zero-to-green.html
          else
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
          fi

          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Download Artifacts
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets

      - name: Recompute SHA256SUMS
        run: shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf > assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*
```

    directory: "/"

      interval: "weekly"
  - package-ecosystem: "npm"
    directory: "/"
    schedule:
      interval: "weekly"
```

nvm use 20

### Final GitHub Actions Workflow with UTC env and Dependabot Configuration:
```yaml
name: build-pdf
on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    tags: [ 'v*' ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

concurrency:
  group: ${{ github.workflow }}-${{ github.ref }}
  cancel-in-progress: true

permissions:
  contents: write

env:
  TZ: UTC

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'

      - name: Cache npm
        uses: actions/cache@v4
        with:
          path: ~/.npm
          key: ${{ runner.os }}-node-${{ hashFiles('**/package-lock.json') }}
          restore-keys: |
            ${{ runner.os }}-node-

      - name: Install Puppeteer
        run: npm ci

      - name: Update footer version/date
        if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
        run: |
          VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
          DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
          sed -i.bak -E "s/Zero-to-Green • v[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+){0,2} • [0-9-]+/Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}/" src/zero-to-green.html

      - name: Build PDFs (Letter/A4/Dark)
        run: |
          mkdir -p assets
          # Letter build script
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            const file = 'file://' + path.join(process.cwd(), 'src/zero-to-green.html');
            await pg.goto(file, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # A4 transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            html = html.replace('size: Letter', 'size: A4')
                       .replace('font: 10pt', 'font: 9.5pt')
                       .replace('1.7fr 1fr', '1.6fr 1fr')
                       .replace('font-size: 8.5pt', 'font-size: 8pt');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-a4.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf',
              format: 'A4',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '12mm',
                right: '12mm',
                bottom: '12mm',
                left: '12mm'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # Dark transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
            html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-dark.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

          # Page size
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"

          # Footer
          if [[ "${GITHUB_REF}" == refs/tags/v* ]]; then
            VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
            DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}" src/zero-to-green.html
          else
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
          fi

          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Download Artifacts
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets

      - name: Recompute SHA256SUMS
        run: shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf > assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*
```

### Include Dependabot Configuration for Automated Updates:

  - package-ecosystem: "github-actions"
    directory: "/"

  - package-ecosystem: "npm"

    schedule:
      interval: "weekly"

            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-dark.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"

          # Footer
          if [[ "${GITHUB_REF}" == refs/tags/v* ]]; then
            VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
            DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}" src/zero-to-green.html
          else
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
          fi

          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Download Artifacts
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets

      - name: Recompute SHA256SUMS
        run: shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf > assets/SHA256SUMS

      - name: Add SHA256SUMS to Release Notes
        run: |
          echo "## SHA256SUMS" > release_notes.md
          cat assets/SHA256SUMS >> release_notes.md
          echo "" >> release_notes.md

      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*
          body-path: release_notes.md
```

**Title:** v1.0.1 — CI hardening, InterSubset embedding, grayscale dark theme, docs + community

**Summary:**
- Hardens CI (build + verify + release), embeds InterSubset (OFL-compliant) to pin rendering, tunes dark theme for B/W printing, and adds docs/community scaffolding.

**Changes:**
- **CI:**
  - Build Letter/A4/Dark, verify page count/size, dynamic footer bump from tag (UTC), generate SHA256SUMS, upload assets.
  - npm cache enabled; Node 20 pinned via .nvmrc; package-lock.json committed.
- **Typography:**
  - Embed InterSubset (base64 WOFF2) via @font-face; updated --font to prefer 'InterSubset'.
  - Added fonts/OFL.txt (SIL OFL 1.1).
- **Theme:**
  - Grayscale-optimized dark palette; footer uses var(--muted).
- **Docs:**
  - README badge + integrity snippet; SECURITY.md; CODE_OF_CONDUCT.md (Covenant 2.1); CONTRIBUTING.md; issue templates.
  - .gitattributes and .gitignore updates.

**Compliance:**
- Inter font licensed under SIL OFL 1.1; derivative name “InterSubset” used to avoid RFN conflicts; full OFL text included.

**Testing:**
- **Local:** npm run build:all; validated single-page PDFs, correct page sizes, footer present, distinct SHA-256.
- **CI:** Workflow runs on PR main; on tag v1.0.1 will bump footer and publish artifacts.

**Screenshots/Artifacts:**
- Attach header and mid-page screenshots if desired, or paste pdfinfo outputs.

**Release plan:**
- Merge → tag v1.0.1 → CI publishes assets + SHA256SUMS.
- Release notes include 3 SHA-256 hashes.

**Reviewer checklist:**
- [ ] README badge OWNER/REPO resolved
- [ ] SECURITY contact set
- [ ] fonts/OFL.txt present
- [ ] InterSubset embedded and used in --font
- [ ] CI verify step passes (page count/size/footer, SHA256SUMS)
- [ ] PDFs remain one page; sizes reasonable.

**Handy commands for the reviewer:**
- **Build locally:**
  ```bash
  nvm use 20 && npm ci && npm run build:all
  ```

- **Verify:**
  ```bash
  sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
  pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf | grep -E "Pages|Page size"
  shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS
  test "$(wc -l < assets/SHA256SUMS)" = "3"
  ```

- **Tag and release:**

  git push --tags
  ```

### gpt-5

Looks excellent. The unified workflow now covers pushes, PRs, and tags; UTC, concurrency, permissions, npm cache keyed with Node 20, dynamic footer bump, verification, SHA256SUMS, and release body are all in place.

Two final, optional micro-tweaks (non-blocking):
- Parameterize Node version in the cache key to avoid hardcoding:
  - uses: actions/setup-node@v4 with node-version: '20'
  - cache key: ${{ runner.os }}-node-${{ steps.node.outputs.node-version }}-${{ hashFiles('**/package-lock.json') }}
  Or keep “20” as you have for predictability.
- Add a quick integrity check in the release job to ensure the recomputed SHA256SUMS matches the build job’s (if you also upload the build’s SHA256SUMS):
  - diff -u assets/SHA256SUMS <(shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf) || exit 1

Otherwise, you’re ready to open the v1.0.1 PR. Share the link when it’s live, and I’ll do a line-by-line review plus a sanity check on the built PDFs and hashes.
