### 4o

Let's incorporate your final suggestions for robustness and proceed to open the PR.

### Final Unified Workflow with Parameterized Node Version and Integrity Check:

#### Final GitHub Actions Workflow:
```yaml
name: build-pdf
on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    tags: [ 'v*' ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

concurrency:
  group: ${{ github.workflow }}-${{ github.ref }}
  cancel-in-progress: true

permissions:
  contents: write

env:
  TZ: UTC

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: build
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - id: node
        name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'
          check-latest: true

      - name: Cache npm
        uses: actions/cache@v4
        with:
          path: ~/.npm
          key: ${{ runner.os }}-node-${{ steps.node.outputs.node-version }}-${{ hashFiles('**/package-lock.json') }}
          restore-keys: |
            ${{ runner.os }}-node-${{ steps.node.outputs.node-version }}-

      - name: Install Puppeteer
        run: npm ci

      - name: Update footer version/date
        if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
        run: |
          VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
          DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
          sed -i.bak -E "s/Zero-to-Green • v[0-9]+(\.[0-9]+){0,2} • [0-9-]+/Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}/" src/zero-to-green.html

      - name: Build PDFs (Letter/A4/Dark)
        run: |
          mkdir -p assets
          # Letter build script
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            const file = 'file://' + path.join(process.cwd(), 'src/zero-to-green.html');
            await pg.goto(file, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # A4 transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            html = html.replace('size: Letter', 'size: A4')
                       .replace('font: 10pt', 'font: 9.5pt')
                       .replace('1.7fr 1fr', '1.6fr 1fr')
                       .replace('font-size: 8.5pt', 'font-size: 8pt');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-a4.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf',
              format: 'A4',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '12mm',
                right: '12mm',
                bottom: '12mm',
                left: '12mm'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS
          # Dark transform + build
          node - <<'JS'
          const p = require('puppeteer'); const fs = require('fs'); const path = require('path');
          (async () => {
            let html = fs.readFileSync('src/zero-to-green.html', 'utf8');
            const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
            html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-dark.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,
              margin: {
                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'
              }
            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

          # Page size
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf      | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf   | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "595 x 842 pts"
          pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf | awk -F: '/Page size/{print $2}' | grep -q "612 x 792 pts"

          # Footer
          if [[ "${GITHUB_REF}" == refs/tags/v* ]]; then
            VERSION="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
            DATE="$(date -u +%F)"
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • ${VERSION} • ${DATE}" src/zero-to-green.html
          else
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
          fi

          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Download Artifacts
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets

      - name: Recompute SHA256SUMS
        run: shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf > assets/SHA256SUMS

      - name: Integrity Check for SHA256SUMS
        run: diff -u assets/SHA256SUMS <(shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf) || exit 1

      - name: Add SHA256SUMS to Release Notes
        run: |
          echo "## SHA256SUMS" > release_notes.md
          cat assets/SHA256SUMS >> release_notes.md
          echo "" >> release_notes.md

      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*
          body-path: release_notes.md
```

  - package-ecosystem: "github-actions"

---

### gpt-5

Looks great. Two quick fixes before you open the PR:

1) Cache key output variable
- actions/setup-node@v4 doesn’t expose node-version as an output. Your cache key may end up missing that segment. Keep it explicit:
  key: ${{ runner.os }}-node-20-${{ hashFiles('**/package-lock.json') }}
  restore-keys: |
    ${{ runner.os }}-node-20-

2) Release integrity check (don’t overwrite before diff)
- You currently overwrite assets/SHA256SUMS, then diff it against a fresh computation—this always passes. Compare against the artifact’s original file first:
  - name: Integrity Check for SHA256SUMS
    run: |
      shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf > /tmp/SHA256SUMS
      diff -u assets/SHA256SUMS /tmp/SHA256SUMS
- If you still want to regenerate after verification, you can copy /tmp/SHA256SUMS back to assets/SHA256SUMS afterward.

With those two tweaks, you’re good to open the v1.0.1 PR. Share the link when it’s live, and I’ll do the line-by-line review and sanity-check the PDFs and hashes.

### GitHub Actions Workflow:
```yaml

                bottom: '12mm',
                left: '12mm'

            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

            const dark = ":root{--bg:#0f1116;--text:#e7eaf0;--muted:#a7afc0;--brand:#7aa8e8;--secondary:#4b8bd9;--accent-bg:#171a21;--code-bg:#151923;--border:#2a3140;} .sidebar{border-color:var(--border);} .pill{color:var(--muted);border-color:var(--border);}";
            html = html.replace('</style>', dark + '</style>');
            const tmp = path.join('/tmp', 'zero-to-green-dark.html');
            fs.writeFileSync(tmp, html);
            const b = await p.launch({args:['--no-sandbox']});
            const pg = await b.newPage();
            await pg.goto('file://' + tmp, { waitUntil:'networkidle0' });
            await pg.pdf({
              path: 'assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf',
              format: 'Letter',
              printBackground: true,

                top: '0.5in',
                right: '0.5in',
                bottom: '0.5in',
                left: '0.5in'

            });
            await b.close();
          })();
          JS

      - name: Verify PDFs and hashes
        run: |
          sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y poppler-utils
          ls -l assets/Zero-to-Green*.pdf

          # Page count
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green.pdf        | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-A4.pdf     | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"
          test "$(pdfinfo assets/Zero-to-Green-Dark.pdf   | awk -F: '/Pages/{print $2}' | xargs)" = "1"

          else
            grep -q "Zero-to-Green • v1.0 • 2025-10-26" src/zero-to-green.html
          fi

          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf | tee assets/SHA256SUMS

      - uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets/*

  release:
    needs: build
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Download Artifacts
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: zero-to-green-pdfs
          path: assets

      - name: Integrity Check for SHA256SUMS

          shasum -a 256 assets/*.pdf > /tmp/SHA256SUMS
          diff -u assets/SHA256SUMS /tmp/SHA256SUMS || exit 1

      - name: Add SHA256SUMS to Release Notes
        run: |
          echo "## SHA256SUMS" > release_notes.md
          cat /tmp/SHA256SUMS >> release_notes.md
          echo "" >> release_notes.md

      - uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2
        with:
          files: assets/*
          body-path: release_notes.md
```

### Update Dependabot Configuration:
```yaml
.github/dependabot.yml
```
```yaml
version: 2
updates:
  - package-ecosystem: "github-actions"
    directory: "/"
    schedule:
      interval: "weekly"
  - package-ecosystem: "npm"
    directory: "/"
    schedule:
      interval: "weekly"
```

Great—PR opened. I can’t access the link directly, but based on everything we’ve built, here’s a focused review plan and a few non-blocking nits to consider before merge.

What I’ll look for in the PR (line-by-line)
- Workflow (build-pdf)
  - Triggers: push (main + tags), pull_request (main) — good.
  - Concurrency and permissions present — good.
  - UTC env set globally — good.
  - Cache npm: key pinned to Node 20 + lockfile hash — good.
  - Install via npm ci — good.
  - Footer bump only on tags; regex covers vMAJOR[.MINOR[.PATCH]] — good.
  - Build: Letter/A4/Dark using Puppeteer — good.
  - Verify: pdfinfo checks (page count/size), footer grep (HTML source), SHA256SUMS — good.
  - Artifacts: uploads assets/* (includes PDFs + SHA256SUMS) — good.
  - Release job: downloads artifacts, recomputes hashes for integrity (diff vs build), appends SHA256SUMS to release notes, uploads files — good.

- Source (HTML/CSS)
  - InterSubset @font-face embedded; --font starts with 'InterSubset'; footer uses var(--muted).
  - Dark palette uses grayscale-friendly colors.
  - Footer text present in HTML; no curly quotes lurking.

- Fonts/licensing
  - fonts/OFL.txt included (full SIL OFL 1.1).
  - Family renamed to InterSubset (avoids RFN conflicts).
  - README references OFL (if you added a note).

- Scripts/docs
  - scripts/build-letter.js, build-a4.js, build-dark.js exist and match package.json.
  - README badge OWNER/REPO set; SECURITY email real.
  - CONTRIBUTING, CODE_OF_CONDUCT, templates present; .gitattributes marks PDFs as binary; .gitignore excludes node_modules and built PDFs.

- CI run artifacts
  - Three PDFs exist, each 1 page.
  - Sizes: Letter 612x792 pts; A4 595x842 pts; Dark 612x792 pts.
  - SHA-256 hashes distinct; integrity diff passes.
  - Release job scoped to tags only, uses GITHUB_TOKEN with contents: write.

Nice-to-have (non-blocking, optional)
- Speed up CI by caching Chromium between runs:
  - Add env: PUPPETEER_CACHE_DIR: ~/.cache/puppeteer
  - Cache that directory:
    - uses: actions/cache@v4
      with:
        path: ~/.cache/puppeteer
        key: ${{ runner.os }}-puppeteer-${{ hashFiles('**/package-lock.json') }}
- Pin softprops/action-gh-release@v2 by SHA or a minor release if your org requires strict pinning.
- Consider a small make verify target locally mirroring CI’s pdfinfo checks.

Next steps
- Share the PR link; I’ll do the line-by-line review and scan the CI logs/artifacts.
- After merge, tag v1.0.1; confirm CI publishes three PDFs + SHA256SUMS and that release notes contain the hashes (auto-added by the workflow).
